# <a name="microsoft-graph-permissions-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-104">Microsoft Graph 权限引用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-104">Microsoft Graph permissions reference</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-105">若要使你的应用可访问 Microsoft Graph 中的数据，用户或管理员必须通过同意过程向其授予正确的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-105">For your app to access data in Microsoft Graph, the user or administrator must grant it the correct permissions via a consent process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-106">本主题列出了与每个主要 Microsoft Graph API 集关联的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-106">This topic lists the permissions associated with each major set of Microsoft Graph APIs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-107">它还提供有关如何使用权限的指导。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-107">It also provides guidance about how to use the permissions.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-108">若要阅读有关权限如何工作的更多信息，请参阅[身份验证和授权基础知识](https://docs.microsoft.com/zh-CN/graph/auth/auth-concepts?view=graph-rest-1.0#microsoft-graph-permissions)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-108">To read more about how permissions work, see [Authentication and authorization basics](https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/graph/auth/auth-concepts?view=graph-rest-1.0#microsoft-graph-permissions).</span></span>

## <a name="microsoft-graph-permission-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-109">Microsoft Graph 权限名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-109">Microsoft Graph permission names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p103">Microsoft Graph 权限名称遵循简单模式：_resource.operation.constraint_。例如，_User.Read_ 授予读取已登录用户的配置文件的权限，_User.ReadWrite_ 授予读取和修改已登录用户的配置文件的权限，而 _Mail.Send_ 则授予代表已登录用户发送邮件的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p103">Microsoft Graph permission names follow a simple pattern: _resource.operation.constraint_. For example, _User.Read_ grants permission to read the profile of the signed-in user, _User.ReadWrite_ grants permission to read and modify the profile of the signed-in user, and _Mail.Send_ grants permission to send mail on behalf of the signed-in user.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p104">名称的 _constraint_ 元素决定了你的应用程序在目录中具有的潜在访问范围。Microsoft Graph 当前支持以下约束：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p104">The _constraint_ element of the name determines the potential extent of access your app will have within the directory. Currently Microsoft Graph supports the following constraints:</span></span> 

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p105">**All** 授予应用对目录中指定类型的所有资源执行操作的权限。例如，_User.Read.All_ 可能授予应用读取目录中所有用户的配置文件的特权。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p105">**All** grants permission for the app to perform the operations on all of the resources of the specified type in a directory. For example, _User.Read.All_ potentially grants the app privileges to read the profiles of all of the users in a directory.</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p106">**Shared** 授予该应用对其他用户与已登录用户共享的资源执行操作的权限。此约束主要用于 Outlook 资源，如邮件、日历和联系人。例如，_Mail.Read.Shared_ 授予在已登录用户的邮箱中以及组织中的其他用户与已登录用户共享的邮箱中读取邮件的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p106">**Shared** grants permission for the app to perform the operations on resources that other users have shared with the signed-in user. This constraint is mainly used with Outlook resources like mail, calendars, and contacts. For example, _Mail.Read.Shared_, grants privileges to read mail in the mailbox of the signed-in user as well as mail in mailboxes that other users in the organization have shared with the signed-in user.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p107">**AppFolder** 授予应用在 OneDrive 专用文件夹中读取和写入文件的权限。此约束仅在[文件权限](#files-permissions)上公开，并且仅适用于 Microsoft 帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p107">**AppFolder** grants permission for the app to read and write files in a dedicated folder in OneDrive. This constraint is only exposed on [Files permissions](#files-permissions) and is only valid for Microsoft accounts.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p108">如果未指定**任何约束**，则应用程序仅限于对已登录用户拥有的资源执行操作。例如，_User.Read_ 仅授予读取已登录用户的配置文件的特权，_Mail.Read_ 仅授予读取已登录用户邮箱中的邮件的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p108">If **no constraint** is specified the app is limited to performing the operations on the resources owned by the signed-in user. For example, _User.Read_ grants privileges to read the profile of the signed-in user only, and _Mail.Read_ grants permission to read only mail in the mailbox of the signed-in user.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-123">**注意**：在委托场景中，授予应用的有效权限可能受到组织中已登录用户的特权的限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-123">**Note**: In delegated scenarios, the effective permissions granted to your app may be constrained by the privileges of the signed-in user in the organization.</span></span>

## <a name="microsoft-accounts-and-work-or-school-accounts"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-124">Microsoft 帐户和工作或学校帐户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-124">Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-125">并非所有权限都适用于 Microsoft 帐户和工作或学校帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-125">Not all permissions are valid for both Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-126">你可以检查每个权限组的**支持的 Microsoft 帐户**列，以确定特定权限是否对 Microsoft 帐户和/或工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-126">You can check the **Microsoft Account Supported** column for each permission group to determine whether a specific permission is valid for Microsoft accounts, work or school accounts, or both.</span></span>

## <a name="user-and-group-search-limitations-for-guest-users-in-organizations"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-127">组织中来宾用户的用户和组搜索限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-127">User and group search limitations for guest users in organizations</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-128">用户和组搜索功能允许应用通过对 `/users` 或 `/groups` 资源集（例如 `https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/users`）执行查询来搜索组织目录中的任何用户或组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-128">User and group search capabilities allow the app to search for any user or group in an organization's directory by performing queries against the `/users` or `/groups` resource set (for example, `https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/users`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-129">管理员和用户都可以使用此功能；但来宾用户不可以。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-129">Both administrators and users have this capability; however, guest users do not.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-130">如果登录用户是来宾用户，应用程序可以读取特定用户或组的配置文件（例如，`https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/users/241f22af-f634-44c0-9a15-c8cd2cea5531`），具体视应用程序获得的授权而定；不过，不能对可能返回多个资源的 `/users` 或 `/groups` 资源集执行查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-130">If the signed-in user is a guest user, depending on the permissions an app has been granted, it can read the profile of a specific user or group (for example, `https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/users/241f22af-f634-44c0-9a15-c8cd2cea5531`); however, it cannot perform queries against the `/users` or `/groups` resource set that potentially return more than a single resource.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-131">借助授予的适当权限，应用程序可以读取用户或组的配置文件，具体是通过导航属性中的链接获取；例如，`/users/{id}/directReports` 或 `/groups/{id}/members`。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-131">With the appropriate permissions, the app can read the profiles of users or groups that it obtains by following links in navigation properties; for example, `/users/{id}/directReports` or `/groups/{id}/members`.</span></span>

---

## <a name="access-reviews-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-132">访问评审权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-132">Access reviews permissions</span></span>

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-149">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-149">Application permissions</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-150">权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-150">Permission</span></span>    |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-151">显示字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-151">Display String</span></span>   |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-152">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-152">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-153">需经过管理员同意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-153">Admin Consent Required</span></span> |

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-158">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-158">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-159">_AccessReview.Read.All_ 和 _AccessReview.ReadWrite.All_ 仅对工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-159">_AccessReview.Read.All_ and _AccessReview.ReadWrite.All_ are valid only for work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-160">对于通过委派权限读取组或应用的访问评审的应用，登录的用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员、安全管理员、安全读取者或用户管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-160">For an app with delegated permissions to read access reviews of a group or app, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator, Security Administrator, Security Reader or User Administrator.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-161">对于通过委派权限读取组或应用的访问评审的应用，登录的用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员或用户管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-161">For an app with delegated permissions to write access reviews of a group or app, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator or User Administrator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-162">对于通过委派权限读取 Azure AD 角色的访问评审的应用，登录的用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员、安全管理员、安全读取者或特权角色管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-162">For an app with delegated permissions to read access reviews of an Azure AD role, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator, Security Administrator, Security Reader or Privileged Role Administrator.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-163">对于通过委派权限写入 Azure AD 角色的访问评审的应用，登录的用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员或特权角色管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-163">For an app with delegated permissions to write access reviews of an Azure AD role, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator or Privileged Role Administrator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-164">若要详细了解管理员角色，请参阅[在 Azure Active Directory 中分配管理员角色](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-164">For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

## <a name="appcatalog-resource-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-165">AppCatalog 资源权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-165">AppCatalog resource permissions</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-166">委派权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-166">Delegated permissions</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-167">权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-167">Permission</span></span>    |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-168">显示字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-168">Display String</span></span>   |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-169">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-169">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-170">需经过管理员同意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-170">Admin Consent Required</span></span> |
|:-----------------------------|:-----------------------------------------|:-----------------|:-----------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-171">_AppCatalog.ReadWrite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-171">_AppCatalog.ReadWrite.All_</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-172">读取和写入所有应用目录</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-172">Read and write to all app catalogs</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-173">允许应用在应用目录中创建、读取、更新和删除应用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-173">Allows the app to create, read, update, and delete apps in the app catalogs.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-174">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-174">Yes</span></span> |

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-179">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-179">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-180">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-180">Delegated</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-181">_AppCatalog.ReadWrite.All_：[：列出目录中的所有应用程序](/graph/api/teamsapp-list?view=graph-rest-beta) (`GET /beta/appCatalogs/teamsApps`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-181">_AppCatalog.ReadWrite.All_: [List all applications in catalog](/graph/api/teamsapp-list?view=graph-rest-beta) (`GET /beta/appCatalogs/teamsApps`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-182">_AppCatalog.ReadWrite.All_：[发布一个应用](/graph/api/teamsapp-publish?view=graph-rest-beta) (`POST /beta/appCatalogs/teamsApps`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-182">_AppCatalog.ReadWrite.All_: [Publish an app](/graph/api/teamsapp-publish?view=graph-rest-beta) (`POST /beta/appCatalogs/teamsApps`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-183">_AppCatalog.ReadWrite.All_：[更新某个已发布的应用](/graph/api/teamsapp-update?view=graph-rest-beta) (`PATCH /beta/appCatalogs/teamsApps/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-183">_AppCatalog.ReadWrite.All_: [Update a published app](/graph/api/teamsapp-update?view=graph-rest-beta) (`PATCH /beta/appCatalogs/teamsApps/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-184">_AppCatalog.ReadWrite.All_：[删除某个已发布的应用](/graph/api/teamsapp-delete?view=graph-rest-beta) (`DELETE /beta/appCatalogs/teamsApps/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-184">_AppCatalog.ReadWrite.All_: [Remove a published app](/graph/api/teamsapp-delete?view=graph-rest-beta) (`DELETE /beta/appCatalogs/teamsApps/{id}`)</span></span>

## <a name="application-resource-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-187">应用程序资源权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-187">Application resource permissions</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-188">委派权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-188">Delegated permissions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-189">无。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-189">None.</span></span>

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-190">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-190">Application permissions</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-191">权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-191">Permission</span></span>    |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-192">显示字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-192">Display String</span></span>   |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-193">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-193">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-194">需经过管理员同意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-194">Admin Consent Required</span></span> |
|:-----------------------------|:-----------------------------------------|:-----------------|:-----------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-195">_Application.ReadWrite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-195">_Application.ReadWrite.All_</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-196">读取和写入所有应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-196">Read and write all apps</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-197">允许调用应用在没有登录用户的情况下创建和管理（读取、更新、更新应用程序密码和删除）应用程序和服务主体。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-197">Allows the calling app to create, and manage (read, update, update application secrets and delete) applications and service principals without a signed-in user.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-198">不允许管理对用户或组的同意授权或应用程序分配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-198">Does not allow management of consent grants or application assignments to users or groups.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-199">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-199">Yes</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-200">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-200">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-201">管理此应用创建或拥有的应用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-201">Manage apps that this app creates or owns</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-202">允许调用应用在没有登录用户的情况下创建其他应用程序和服务主体，以及完全管理这些应用程序和服务主体（读取、更新、更新应用程序密码和删除）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-202">Allows the calling app to create other applications and service principals, and fully manage those applications and service principals (read, update, update application secrets and delete), without a signed-in user.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-203">它无法更新任何不是其所有者的应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-203">It cannot update any applications that it is not an owner of.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-204">不允许管理对用户或组的同意授权或应用程序分配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-204">Does not allow management of consent grants or application assignments to users or groups.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-205">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-205">Yes</span></span> |

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-206">备注</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-206">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-207">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_ 权限允许与 _Application.ReadWrite.All_ 相同的操作，只不过前者只允许对调用应用充当所有者的应用程序和服务主体执行这些操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-207">The _Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_ permission allows the same operations as _Application.ReadWrite.All_ except that the former allows these operations only on applications and service principals that the calling app is an owner of.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-208">所有权由目标 [application](/graph/api/application-list-owners?view=graph-rest-beta) 或 [service principal](/graph/api/serviceprincipal-list-owners?view=graph-rest-beta) 资源上的 `owners` 导航属性指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-208">Ownership is indicated by the `owners` navigation property on the target [application](/graph/api/application-list-owners?view=graph-rest-beta) or [service principal](/graph/api/serviceprincipal-list-owners?view=graph-rest-beta) resource.</span></span>
> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-209">注意：使用 _Application.Read Write.Owned by_ 权限调用 `GET /applications` 以列出应用程序将失败，并显示 403。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-209">NOTE: Using the _Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_ permission to call `GET /applications` to list applications will fail with a 403.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-210">请改为使用 `GET servicePrincipals/{id}/ownedObjects` 列出调用应用程序充当所有者的应用程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-210">Instead use `GET servicePrincipals/{id}/ownedObjects` to list the applications owned by the calling application.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-211">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-211">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-212">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-212">Delegated</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-213">无。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-213">None.</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-214">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-214">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-215">_Application.ReadWrite.All_：列出所有应用程序 (`GET /beta/applications`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-215">_Application.ReadWrite.All_: List all applications (`GET /beta/applications`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-216">_Application.ReadWrite.All_：删除服务主体 (`DELETE /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-216">_Application.ReadWrite.All_: Delete a service principal (`DELETE /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-217">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_：创建应用程序 (`POST /beta/applications`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-217">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_: Create an application (`POST /beta/applications`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-218">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_：列出调用应用程序拥有的所有应用程序 (`GET /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}/ownedObjects`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-218">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_: List all applications owned by the the calling application (`GET /beta/servicePrincipals/{id}/ownedObjects`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-219">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_：向拥有的应用程序添加另一个所有者 (`POST /applications/{id}/owners/$ref`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-219">_Application.ReadWrite.OwnedBy_: Add another owner to an owned application (`POST /applications/{id}/owners/$ref`).</span></span>  
> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-220">注意：这可能需要其他权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-220">NOTE: This may require additional permissions.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-258">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-258">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-259">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-259">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-260">_Bookings.Read.All_：获取为租户创建的预订业务集合的 ID 和名称 (`GET /bookingBusinesses`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-260">_Bookings.Read.All_: Get the ID and names of the collection of Bookings businesses that has been created for a tenant (`GET /bookingBusinesses`).</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-263">_Bookings.Manage_：使此业务的日程安排页对外部客户可用 (`POST /bookingBusinesses/{id}/publish`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-263">_Bookings.Manage_: Make the scheduling page of this business available to external customers (`POST /bookingBusinesses/{id}/publish`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-292">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-292">Application permissions</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-293">权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-293">Permission</span></span>    |<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-294">显示字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-294">Display String</span></span>   |<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-295">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-295">Description</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-296">需经过管理员同意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-296">Admin Consent Required</span></span> |
|:-----------------------------|:-----------------------------------------|:-----------------|:-----------------|
|<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-297">_Calendars.Read_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-297">_Calendars.Read_</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-298">读取所有邮箱中的日历</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-298">Read calendars in all mailboxes</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-299">允许应用在没有登录用户的情况下读取所有日历的事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-299">Allows the app to read events of all calendars without a signed-in user.</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-300">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-300">Yes</span></span> |

<br/>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-305">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-305">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-306">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-306">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-307">_Calendars.Read_：获取从 2017 年 4 月 23 日到 2017 年 4 月 29 日用户日历中的事件 (`GET /me/calendarView?startDateTime=2017-04-23T00:00:00&endDateTime=2017-04-29T00:00:00`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-307">_Calendars.Read_: Get events on the user's calendar between April 23, 2017 and April 29, 2017 (`GET /me/calendarView?startDateTime=2017-04-23T00:00:00&endDateTime=2017-04-29T00:00:00`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-308">_Calendars.Read.Shared_：查找所有与会者都均有空参加的会议时间 (`POST /users/{id|userPrincipalName}/findMeetingTimes`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-308">_Calendars.Read.Shared_: Find meeting times where all attendees are available (`POST /users/{id|userPrincipalName}/findMeetingTimes`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-309">_Calendars.ReadWrite_：将事件添加到用户日历 (`POST /me/events`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-309">_Calendars.ReadWrite_: Add an event to the user's calendar (`POST /me/events`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-310">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-310">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-311">_Calendars.Read_：在 bob@contoso.com 组织整理的会议室日历中查找事件 (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/events?$filter=organizer/emailAddress/address eq 'bob@contoso.com'`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-311">_Calendars.Read_: Find events in a conference room's calendar organized by bob@contoso.com (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/events?$filter=organizer/emailAddress/address eq 'bob@contoso.com'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-312">_Calendars.Read_：列出 5 月份用户日历上的所有事件 (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/calendarView?startDateTime=2017-05-01T00:00:00&endDateTime=2017-06-01T00:00:00`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-312">_Calendars.Read_: List all events on a user's calendar for the month of May (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/calendarView?startDateTime=2017-05-01T00:00:00&endDateTime=2017-06-01T00:00:00`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-313">_Calendars.ReadWrite_：将获准休假事件添加到用户日历 (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/events`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-313">_Calendars.ReadWrite_: Add an event to a user's calendar for approved time off  (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/events`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-314">_Calendars.Send_：发送邮件 (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/sendCalendars`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-314">_Calendars.Send_: Send a message (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/sendCalendars`).</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-315">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-315">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-347">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-347">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-348">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-348">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-349">_Calls.Initiate.All_：从应用程序向组织中的某个用户发起对等通话 (`POST /beta/app/calls`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-349">_Calls.Initiate.All_: Make a peer-to-peer call from the application to a user in the organization (`POST /beta/app/calls`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-350">_Calls.InitiateGroupCall.All_：从应用程序向组织中的一组用户发起组通话 (`POST /beta/app/calls`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-350">_Calls.InitiateGroupCall.All_: Make a group call from the application to a group of users in the organization (`POST /beta/app/calls`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-351">_Calls.JoinGroupCall.All_：从应用程序加入组通话或联机会议 (`POST /beta/app/calls`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-351">_Calls.JoinGroupCall.All_: Join a group call or online meeting from the application (`POST /beta/app/calls`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-352">_Calls.JoinGroupCallasGuest.All_：从应用程序加入组通话或联机会议，但应用程序在会议中仅具有来宾特权 (`POST /beta/app/calls`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-352">_Calls.JoinGroupCallasGuest.All_: Join a group call or online meeting from the application, but the application only has guest privileges in the meeting (`POST /beta/app/calls`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-353">_Calls.AccessMedia.All_：创建或加入某个通话，且应用将能够直接访问该通话中的参与者媒体数据流 (`POST /beta/app/calls`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-353">_Calls.AccessMedia.All_: Create or Join a call and the app gets direct access to participant media streams in the call (`POST /beta/app/calls`).</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-354">**注意：** 有关请求示例，请参阅[创建通话](/graph/api/application-post-calls?view=graph-rest-beta)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-354">**Note:** For request examples, see to [Create call](/graph/api/application-post-calls?view=graph-rest-beta).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-355">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-355">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-425">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-425">Example usage</span></span>
#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-426">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-426">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-427">_Contacts.Read_：从登录用户的一个顶层联系人文件夹读取联系人 (`GET /me/contactfolders/{Id}/contacts/{id}`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-427">_Contacts.Read_: Read a contact from one of the top-level contact folders of the signed-in user (`GET /me/contactfolders/{Id}/contacts/{id}`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-428">_Contacts.ReadWrite_：更新登录用户的一个联系人的联系人照片 (`PUT /me/contactfolders/{contactFolderId}/contacts/{id}/photo/$value`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-428">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Update the contact photo of one of the signed-in user's contacts (`PUT /me/contactfolders/{contactFolderId}/contacts/{id}/photo/$value`).</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-429">_Contacts.ReadWrite_：将联系人添加到登录用户的根文件夹 (`POST /me/contacts`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-429">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Add contacts to the root folder of the signed-in user (`POST /me/contacts`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-430">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-430">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-431">_Contacts.Read_：从组织中任意用户的一个顶层联系人文件夹读取联系人 (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/contactfolders/{Id}/contacts/{id}`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-431">_Contacts.Read_: Read contacts from one of the top-level contact folders of any user in the organization (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/contactfolders/{Id}/contacts/{id}`).</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-432">_Contacts.ReadWrite_：更新组织中任意用户的所有联系人的照片 (`PUT /user/{id | userPrincipalName}/contactfolders/{contactFolderId}/contacts/{id}/photo/$value`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-432">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Update the photo for any contact of any user in an organization (`PUT /user/{id | userPrincipalName}/contactfolders/{contactFolderId}/contacts/{id}/photo/$value`).</span></span> 
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-433">_Contacts.ReadWrite_：将联系人添加到组织中任意用户的根文件夹 (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/contacts`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-433">_Contacts.ReadWrite_: Add contacts to the root folder of any user in the organization (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/contacts`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-434">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-434">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-500">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-500">Application permissions</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-501">权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-501">Permission</span></span>    |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-502">显示字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-502">Display String</span></span>   |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-503">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-503">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-504">需经过管理员同意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-504">Admin Consent Required</span></span> |
|:-----------------------------|:-----------------------------------------|:-----------------|:-----------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-505">_Directory.Read.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-505">_Directory.Read.All_</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-506">读取目录数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-506">Read directory data</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-507">允许应用在没有登录用户的情况下读取组织目录中的数据（如用户、组和应用）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-507">Allows the app to read data in your organization's directory, such as users, groups and apps, without a signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-508">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-508">Yes</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-509">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-509">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-510">读取和写入目录数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-510">Read and write directory data</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p128">允许应用在没有登录用户的情况下读取和写入组织目录中的数据（如用户和组）。不允许删除用户或组。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p128">Allows the app to read and write data in your organization's directory, such as users, and groups, without a signed-in user. Does not allow user or group deletion.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-513">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-513">Yes</span></span> |

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-514">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-514">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-515">Directory 权限提供访问目录资源（如组织中的 [User](/graph/api/resources/user?view=graph-rest-1.0)、[Group](/graph/api/resources/group?view=graph-rest-1.0) 和 [Device](/graph/api/resources/device?view=graph-rest-1.0)）的最高级特权。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-515">Directory permissions provide the highest level of privilege for accessing directory resources such as [User](/graph/api/resources/user?view=graph-rest-1.0), [Group](/graph/api/resources/group?view=graph-rest-1.0), and [Device](/graph/api/resources/device?view=graph-rest-1.0) in an organization.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-516">它们还专门控制对其他目录资源的访问，如[组织联系人](/graph/api/resources/orgcontact?view=graph-rest-beta)、[架构扩展 API](/graph/api/resources/schemaextension?view=graph-rest-beta)、[Privileged Identity Management (PIM) API](/graph/api/resources/privilegedidentitymanagement-root?view=graph-rest-beta)，以及 v1.0 和 beta API 参考文档中 **Azure Active Directory** 节点下列出的许多资源和 API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-516">They also exclusively control access to other directory resources like: [organizational contacts](/graph/api/resources/orgcontact?view=graph-rest-beta), [schema extension APIs](/graph/api/resources/schemaextension?view=graph-rest-beta), [Privileged Identity Management (PIM) APIs](/graph/api/resources/privilegedidentitymanagement-root?view=graph-rest-beta), as well as many of the resources and APIs listed under the **Azure Active Directory** node in the v1.0 and beta API reference documentation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-517">其中包括管理单元、目录角色、目录设置、策略等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-517">These include administrative units, directory roles, directory settings, policy, and many more.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-518">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_ 权限可授予以下特权：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-518">The _Directory.ReadWrite.All_ permission grants the following privileges:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-519">完全读取所有目录资源（包括声明属性和导航属性）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-519">Full read of all directory resources (both declared properties and navigation properties)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-520">创建和更新用户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-520">Create and update users</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-521">禁用和启用用户（而不是公司管理员）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-521">Disable and enable users (but not company administrator)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-522">设置用户可选安全 ID（而不是管理员）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-522">Set user alternative security id (but not administrators)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-523">创建和更新组</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-523">Create and update groups</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-524">管理组成员</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-524">Manage group memberships</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-525">更新组所有者</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-525">Update group owner</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-526">管理许可证分配</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-526">Manage license assignments</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-527">在应用程序上定义架构扩展</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-527">Define schema extensions on applications</span></span>
> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-528">**注意**：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-528">**Note**:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-529">无权重置用户密码</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-529">No rights to reset user passwords</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-530">无权删除资源（包括用户或组）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-530">No rights to delete resources (including users or groups)</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-531">特别排除创建或更新以上未列出的资源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-531">Specifically excludes create or update for resources not listed above.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-532">这包括：application、oAauth2Permissiongrant、appRoleAssignment、device、servicePrincipal、organization、domains等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-532">This includes: application, oAauth2Permissiongrant, appRoleAssignment, device, servicePrincipal, organization, domains, and so on.</span></span>
 

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-533">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-533">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-534">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-534">Delegated</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-535">_Directory.Read.All_：列出组织中的所有管理单元 (`GET /beta/administrativeUnits`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-535">_Directory.Read.All_: List all administrative units in an organization (`GET /beta/administrativeUnits`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-536">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_：将成员添加到目录角色 (`POST /directoryRoles/{id}/members/$ref`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-536">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_: Add members to a directory role (`POST /directoryRoles/{id}/members/$ref`)</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-537">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-537">Application</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-538">_Directory.Read.All_：列出用户的所有成员资格，包括目录角色和管理单元 (`GET /beta/users/{id}/memberOf`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-538">_Directory.Read.All_: List all memberships of a user, including directory roles and administrative units (`GET /beta/users/{id}/memberOf`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-539">_Directory.Read.All_：列出所有组成员，包括服务主体 (`GET /beta/groups/{id}/members`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-539">_Directory.Read.All_: List all group members, including service principals (`GET /beta/groups/{id}/members`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-540">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_：向组添加所有者 (`POST /groups/{id}/owners/$ref`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-540">_Directory.ReadWrite.All_: Add an owner to a group (`POST /groups/{id}/owners/$ref`)</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-541">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-541">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-617">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-617">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-618">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-618">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-619">_EduAssignments.Read_：获取登录学生的作业信息 (`GET /education/classes/{id}/assignments/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-619">_EduAssignments.Read_: Get the signed-in student's assignment information (`GET /education/classes/{id}/assignments/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-620">_EduAssignments.ReadWriteBasic_：提交登录学生的作业 (`GET /education/classes/{id}/assignments/{id}submit`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-620">_EduAssignments.ReadWriteBasic_: Submit signed-in student assignment (`GET /education/classes/{id}/assignments/{id}submit`)</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-682">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-682">Remarks</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-683">**注意**：对于个人帐户，Files.Read 和 Files.ReadWrite 还会授予与登录用户共享的文件的访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-683">**Note**: For personal accounts, Files.Read and Files.ReadWrite also grant access to files shared with the signed-in user.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p133">Files.Read.Selected 和 Files.ReadWrite.Selected 委派权限仅在工作或学校帐户上有效，并仅在处理 [Office 365 文件处理程序 (v1.0)](https://msdn.microsoft.com/office/office365/howto/using-cross-suite-apps) 时才公开。它们不应该用来直接调用 Microsoft Graph API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p133">The Files.Read.Selected and Files.ReadWrite.Selected delegated permissions are only valid on work or school accounts and are only exposed for working with [Office 365 file handlers (v1.0)](https://msdn.microsoft.com/office/office365/howto/using-cross-suite-apps). They should not be used for directly calling Microsoft Graph APIs.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-686">Files.ReadWrite.AppFolder 委派权限仅适于个人帐户，并仅用于访问带有 OneDrive [获取特殊文件夹](/graph/api/drive-get-specialfolder?view=graph-rest-1.0) Microsoft Graph API 的[应用程序根特殊文件夹](https://dev.onedrive.com/misc/appfolder.htm)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-686">The Files.ReadWrite.AppFolder delegated permission is only valid for personal accounts and is used for accessing the [App Root special folder](https://dev.onedrive.com/misc/appfolder.htm) with the OneDrive [Get special folder](/graph/api/drive-get-specialfolder?view=graph-rest-1.0) Microsoft Graph API.</span></span>


### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-687">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-687">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-688">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-688">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-689">_Files.Read_：读取登录用户的 OneDrive 中存储的文件 (`GET /me/drive/root/children`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-689">_Files.Read_: Read files stored in the signed-in user's OneDrive (`GET /me/drive/root/children`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-690">_Files.Read.All_：列出与登录用户共享的文件 (`GET /me/drive/root/sharedWithMe`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-690">_Files.Read.All_: Read files shared with the signed-in user (`GET /me/drive/root/sharedWithMe`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-691">_Files.ReadWrite_：在登录用户的 OneDrive 中写入文件 (`PUT /me/drive/root/children/filename.txt/content`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-691">_Files.ReadWrite_: Write a file in the signed-in user's OneDrive (`PUT /me/drive/root/children/filename.txt/content`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-692">_Files.ReadWrite.All_：写入与用户共享的文件 (`PUT /users/rgregg@contoso.com/drive/root/children/file.txt/content`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-692">_Files.ReadWrite.All_: Write a file shared with the user (`PUT /users/rgregg@contoso.com/drive/root/children/file.txt/content`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-693">_Files.ReadWrite.AppFolder_：在 OneDrive 中将文件写入应用程序的文件夹 (`PUT /me/drive/special/approot/children/file.txt/content`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-693">_Files.ReadWrite.AppFolder_: Write files into the app's folder in OneDrive (`PUT /me/drive/special/approot/children/file.txt/content`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-694">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-694">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-706">委派权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-706">Delegated permissions</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-712">_Group.Read.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-712">_Group.Read.All_</span></span> |    <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-713">读取所有组</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-713">Read all groups</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p134">允许应用代表登录用户列出组，并读取其属性以及所有组成员身份。此外，还允许应用读取登录用户可以访问的所有组的日历、 对话、 文件和其他组内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p134">Allows the app to list groups, and to read their properties and all group memberships on behalf of the signed-in user.  Also allows the app to read calendar, conversations, files, and other group content for all groups the signed-in user can access.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-716">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-716">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-717">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-717">No</span></span> |

Additionally allows group owners to manage their groups and allows group members to update group content.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-722">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-722">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-723">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-723">No</span></span> |

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-724">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-724">Application permissions</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-725">权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-725">Permission</span></span>    |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-726">显示字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-726">Display String</span></span>   |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-727">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-727">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-728">需经过管理员同意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-728">Admin Consent Required</span></span> |
|:-----------------------------|:-----------------------------------------|:-----------------|:-----------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-729">_Group.Read.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-729">_Group.Read.All_</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-730">读取所有组</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-730">Read all groups</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-731">允许应用在没有登录用户的情况下读取所有组的成员身份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-731">Allows the app to read memberships for all groups without a signed-in user.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-732"> > *\*注意：** 并非所有组 API 都支持使用仅限应用权限进行访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-732"> > *\*NOTE:** that not all group API supports access using app-only permissions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-733">有关示例，请参阅[已知问题](known-issues.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-733">See [known issues](known-issues.md) for examples.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-734">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-734">Yes</span></span> |

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-742">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-742">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-743">Microsoft 个人帐户不支持组功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-743">Group functionality is not supported on personal Microsoft accounts.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-744">对于 Office 365 组，组权限授予应用对组内容的访问权限；例如对话、文件、注释等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-744">For Office 365 groups, Group permissions grant the app access to the contents of the group; for example, conversations, files, notes, and so on.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p138">应用程序权限对受支持的 API 有一些限制。有关详细信息，请参阅[已知问题](known-issues.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p138">For application permissions, there are some limitations for the APIs that are supported. For more information, see [known issues](known-issues.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p139">在某些情况下，应用可能需要[目录权限](#directory-permissions)才能读取 `member` 和 `memberOf` 等组属性。例如，如果组将一个或多个 [servicePrincipals](/graph/api/resources/serviceprincipal?view=graph-rest-beta) 作为成员，则应用将需要有效权限才能通过授予的其中一个_目录\*_ 权限读取服务主体，否则 Microsoft Graph 将返回错误。（如果是委派权限，已登录用户还需要组织的足够的权限才能读取服务主体。）相同的指导适用于 `memberOf` 属性，该属性可以返回 [administrativeUnits](/graph/api/resources/administrativeunit?view=graph-rest-beta)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p139">In some cases, an app may need [Directory permissions](#directory-permissions) to read some group properties like `member` and `memberOf`. For example, if a group has a one or more [servicePrincipals](/graph/api/resources/serviceprincipal?view=graph-rest-beta) as members, the app will need effective permissions to read service principals through being granted one of the _Directory.\*_ permissions, otherwise Microsoft Graph will return an error. (In the case of delegated permissions, the signed-in user will also need sufficient privileges in the organization to read service principals.) The same guidance applies for the `memberOf` property, which can return [administrativeUnits](/graph/api/resources/administrativeunit?view=graph-rest-beta).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-750">组权限用于控制对 [Microsoft Teams](/graph/api/resources/teams-api-overview) 资源和 API 的访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-750">Group permissions are used to control access to [Microsoft Teams](/graph/api/resources/teams-api-overview) resources and APIs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-751">不支持 Microsoft 个人帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-751">Personal Microsoft accounts are not supported.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p141">组权限也用于控制对 [Microsoft Planner](/graph/api/resources/planner-overview) 资源和 API 的访问权限。Microsoft Planner API 仅支持委派权限，不支持应用程序权限。不支持 Microsoft 个人帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p141">Group permissions are also used to control access to [Microsoft Planner](/graph/api/resources/planner-overview) resources and APIs. Only delegated permissions are supported for Microsoft Planner APIs; application permissions are not supported. Personal Microsoft accounts are not supported.</span></span>


### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-755">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-755">Example usage</span></span>
#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-756">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-756">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-757">_Group.Read.All_：读取登录用户所属的全部 Office 365 组 (`GET /me/memberOf/$/microsoft.graph.group?$filter=groupTypes/any(a:a%20eq%20'unified')`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-757">_Group.Read.All_: Read all Office 365 groups that the signed-in user is a member of (`GET /me/memberOf/$/microsoft.graph.group?$filter=groupTypes/any(a:a%20eq%20'unified')`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-758">_Group.Read.All_：读取诸如对话之类的所有 Office 365 组内容 (`GET /groups/{id}/conversations`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-758">_Group.Read.All_: Read all Office 365 group content like conversations (`GET /groups/{id}/conversations`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-759">_Group.ReadWrite.All_：更新组属性，如照片 (`PUT /groups/{id}/photo/$value`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-759">_Group.ReadWrite.All_: Update group properties, like photo (`PUT /groups/{id}/photo/$value`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-760">_Group.ReadWrite.All_：更新组成员 (`POST /groups/{id}/members/$ref`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-760">_Group.ReadWrite.All_: Update group members (`POST /groups/{id}/members/$ref`).</span></span> 
> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-761">**注意：** 这还要求 _User.ReadBasic.All_ 读取要作为成员添加的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-761">**Note:**: This also requires _User.ReadBasic.All_ to read the user to add as a member.</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-762">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-762">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-763">_Group.Read.All_：查找名称以“Sales”开头的所有组 (`GET /groups?$filter=startswith(displayName,'Sales')`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-763">_Group.Read.All_: Find all groups with name that starts with 'Sales' (`GET /groups?$filter=startswith(displayName,'Sales')`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-764">_Group.ReadWrite.All_：守护程序服务在 Office 365 组日历上新建事件 (`POST /groups/{id}/events`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-764">_Group.ReadWrite.All_: Daemon service creates new events on an Office 365 group's calendar (`POST /groups/{id}/events`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-765">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-765">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

---

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-783">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-783">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-784">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_ 和 _IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ 仅对工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-784">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_ and _IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ are valid only for work or school accounts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-785">登录用户必须分配有全局管理员角色，应用程序才能通过委派权限读取或写入标识提供程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-785">For an app to read or write identity providers with delegated permissions, the signed-in user must be assigned the Global Administrator role.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-786">若要详细了解管理员角色，请参阅[在 Azure Active Directory 中分配管理员角色](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-786">For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-787">示例用法</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-787">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-788">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-788">Delegated</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-789">以下用法对两种委派权限均有效：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-789">The following usages are valid for both delegated permissions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-790">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_：读取在租户中配置的所有标识提供程序 (`GET /beta/identityProviders`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-790">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_: Read all identity providers configured in the tenant (`GET /beta/identityProviders`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-791">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_：读取现有标识提供程序 (`GET /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-791">_IdentityProvider.Read.All_: Read an existing identity provider (`GET /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-792">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_：创建标识提供程序 (`POST /beta/identityProviders`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-792">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ Create an identity provider (`POST /beta/identityProviders`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-793">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_：更新现有标识提供程序 (`PATCH /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-793">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ Update an existing identity provider (`PATCH /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-794">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_：删除现有标识提供程序 (`DELETE /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-794">_IdentityProvider.ReadWrite.All_ Delete an existing identity provider (`DELETE /beta/identityProviders/{id}`)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-795">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-795">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

## <a name="identity-risk-event-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-796">标识风险事件权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-796">Identity Risk Event permissions</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-797">委派权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-797">Delegated permissions</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-798">权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-798">Permission</span></span>    |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-799">显示字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-799">Display String</span></span>   |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-800">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-800">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-801">需经过管理员同意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-801">Admin Consent Required</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-802">支持的 Microsoft 帐户</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-802">Microsoft Account supported</span></span> |
|:----------------|:------------------|:-------------|:-----------------------|:--------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-803">_IdentityRiskEvent.Read.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-803">_IdentityRiskEvent.Read.All_</span></span> |   <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-804">读取标识风险事件信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-804">Read identity risk event information</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-805">允许应用代表登录用户为组织中所有用户读取标识风险事件信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-805">Allows the app to read identity risk event information for all users in your organization on behalf of the signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-806">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-806">Yes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-807">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-807">No</span></span> |

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-808">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-808">Application permissions</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-809">权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-809">Permission</span></span>    |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-810">显示字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-810">Display String</span></span>   |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-811">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-811">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-812">需经过管理员同意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-812">Admin Consent Required</span></span> |

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-817">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-817">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p143">_IdentityRiskEvent.Read.All_ 仅适用于工作或学校帐户。对于通过委派权限读取标识风险信息的应用，登录用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员、安全管理员或安全读者。有关管理员角色的详细信息，请参阅[在 Azure Active Directory 中分配管理员角色](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p143">_IdentityRiskEvent.Read.All_ is valid only for work or school accounts. For an app with delegated permissions to read identity risk information, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator, Security Administrator, or Security Reader. For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-821">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-821">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-and-application"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-822">委派和应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-822">Delegated and Application</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-823">以下用法对委派权限和应用程序权限均有效：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-823">The following usages are valid for both delegated and application permissions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-824">读取为租户中的所有用户所生成的全部风险事件 (`GET /beta/identityRiskEvents`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-824">Read all risk events generated for all users in the tenant (`GET /beta/identityRiskEvents`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-825">读取由 Dorknet 僵尸网络所生成的恶意软件风险事件 (`GET /beta/malwareRiskEvents?$filter=malwareName eq 'Dorkbot'`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-825">Read malware risk events generated by the Dorknet botnet (`GET /beta/malwareRiskEvents?$filter=malwareName eq 'Dorkbot'`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-826">阅读最新的 50 个风险事件 (`GET /beta/identityRiskEvents?$orderBy=riskEventDateTime desc&top=50`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-826">Read most recent 50 risk events (`GET /beta/identityRiskEvents?$orderBy=riskEventDateTime desc&top=50`)</span></span>
 
<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-827">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-827">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-923">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-923">Application permissions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-924">无。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-924">None.</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-925">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-925">Remarks</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-926">**注意：** 使用 Microsoft Graph API 配置 Intune 控件和策略仍需要客户[正确许可](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=839381) Intune 服务。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-926">**Note:** Using the Microsoft Graph APIs to configure Intune controls and policies still requires that the Intune service is [correctly licensed](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=839381) by the customer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-927">这些权限仅对工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-927">These permissions are only valid for work or school accounts.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-928">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-928">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-929">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-929">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-930">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.Read.All_：检查 Intune 订阅的当前状态 (`GET /deviceManagement/subscriptionState`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-930">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.Read.All_: Check the current state of the Intune subscription (`GET /deviceManagement/subscriptionState`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-931">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_：新建条款和条件 (`POST /deviceManagement/termsAndConditions`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-931">_DeviceManagementServiceConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_: Create new Terms and Conditions (`POST /deviceManagement/termsAndConditions`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-932">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.Read.All_：查找设备配置状态 (`GET /deviceManagement/deviceConfigurations/{id}/deviceStatuses`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-932">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.Read.All_: Find the status of a device configuration (`GET /deviceManagement/deviceConfigurations/{id}/deviceStatuses`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-933">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_：向组分配设备符合性策略 (`POST deviceCompliancePolicies/{id}/assign`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-933">_DeviceManagementConfiguration.ReadWrite.All_: Assign a device compliance policy to a group (`POST deviceCompliancePolicies/{id}/assign`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-934">_DeviceManagementApps.Read.All_：查找发布到 Intune 的所有 Windows 应用商店应用 (`GET /deviceAppManagement/mobileApps?$filter=isOf('microsoft.graph.windowsStoreApp')`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-934">_DeviceManagementApps.Read.All_: Find all the Windows Store apps published to Intune (`GET /deviceAppManagement/mobileApps?$filter=isOf('microsoft.graph.windowsStoreApp')`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-935">_DeviceManagementApps.ReadWrite.All_：发布新应用程序 (`POST /deviceAppManagement/mobileApps`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-935">_DeviceManagementApps.ReadWrite.All_: Publish a new application (`POST /deviceAppManagement/mobileApps`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-936">_DeviceManagementRBAC.Read.All_：按名称查找角色分配 (`GET /deviceManagement/roleAssignments?$filter=displayName eq 'My Role Assignment'`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-936">_DeviceManagementRBAC.Read.All_: Find a role assignment by name (`GET /deviceManagement/roleAssignments?$filter=displayName eq 'My Role Assignment'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-937">_DeviceManagementRBAC.ReadWrite.All_：新建自定义角色 (`POST /deviceManagement/roleDefinitions`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-937">_DeviceManagementRBAC.ReadWrite.All_: Create a new custom role (`POST /deviceManagement/roleDefinitions`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-938">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.Read.All_：按名称查找受管理设备 (`GET /managedDevices/?$filter=deviceName eq 'My Device'`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-938">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.Read.All_: Find a managed device by name (`GET /managedDevices/?$filter=deviceName eq 'My Device'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-939">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.ReadWrite.All_：删除受管理设备 (`DELETE /managedDevices/{id}`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-939">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.ReadWrite.All_: Remove a managed device (`DELETE /managedDevices/{id}`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-940">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.PrivilegedOperations.All_：重置用户的受管理设备上的密码 (`POST /managedDevices/{id}/resetPasscode`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-940">_DeviceManagementManagedDevices.PrivilegedOperations.All_: Reset the passcode on a user's managed device (`POST /managedDevices/{id}/resetPasscode`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-941">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-941">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

---

| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1008">_Mail.ReadWrite_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1008">_Mail.ReadWrite_</span></span> |    <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1009">读取和写入所有邮箱中的邮件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1009">Read and write mail in all mailboxes</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p151">允许应用在没有登录用户的情况下创建、读取、更新和删除所有邮箱中的邮件。不包括发送电子邮件的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p151">Allows the app to create, read, update, and delete mail in all mailboxes without a signed-in user. | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1013">_Mail.Send_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1013">_Mail.Send_</span></span> |    <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1014">以任意用户身份发送邮件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1014">Send mail as any user</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1015">允许应用在没有登录用户的情况下以任意用户身份发送邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1015">Allows the app to send mail as any user without a signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1016">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1016">Yes</span></span> | 
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1017">_MailboxSettings.Read_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1017">_MailboxSettings.Read_</span></span> |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1018">读取用户的所有邮箱设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1018">Read all user mailbox settings</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p152">允许应用在没有已登录用户的情况下读取用户邮箱设置。不包括邮件发送权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p152">Allows the app to read user's mailbox settings without a signed-in user. Does not include permission to send mail.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1021">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1021">No</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1022">_MailboxSettings.ReadWrite_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1022">_MailboxSettings.ReadWrite_</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1023">读取和写入所有用户邮箱设置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1023">Read and write all user mailbox settings</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p153">允许应用在没有登录用户的情况下创建、读取、更新和删除用户邮箱设置。不包括邮件发送权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p153">Allows the app to create, read, update, and delete user's mailbox settings without a signed-in user. Does not include permission to send mail.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1026">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1026">Yes</span></span> |

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1027">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1027">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p154">_Mail.Read.Shared_、_Mail.ReadWrite.Shared_ 和 _Mail.Send.Shared_ 仅适用于工作或学校帐户。所有其他权限对于 Microsoft 帐户和工作或学校帐户均有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p154">_Mail.Read.Shared_, _Mail.ReadWrite.Shared_, and _Mail.Send.Shared_ are only valid for work or school accounts. All other permissions are valid for both Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1030">通过 _Mail.Send_ 或 _Mail.Send.Shared_ 权限，应用可以发送邮件并将副本保存到用户的“已发送邮件”文件夹中，即使应用不使用相应的 _Mail.ReadWrite_ 或 _Mail.ReadWrite.Shared _ 权限也是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1030">With the _Mail.Send_ or _Mail.Send.Shared_ permission, an app can send mail and save a copy to the user's Sent Items folder, even if the app does not use a corresponding _Mail.ReadWrite_ or _Mail.ReadWrite.Shared_ permission.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1031">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1031">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1032">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1032">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1033">_Mail.Read_：列出用户收件箱中的邮件，按 `receivedDateTime` 排序 (`GET /me/mailfolders/inbox/messages?$orderby=receivedDateTime DESC`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1033">_Mail.Read_: List messages in the user's inbox, sorted by `receivedDateTime` (`GET /me/mailfolders/inbox/messages?$orderby=receivedDateTime DESC`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1034">_Mail.Read.Shared_：在已与登录用户共享其收件箱的用户收件箱中查找带有附件的所有邮件 (`GET /users{id | userPrincipalName}/mailfolders/inbox/messages?$filter=hasAttachments eq true`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1034">_Mail.Read.Shared_: Find all messages with attachments in a user's inbox that has shared their inbox with the signed-in user (`GET /users{id | userPrincipalName}/mailfolders/inbox/messages?$filter=hasAttachments eq true`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1035">_Mail.ReadWrite_：将邮件标记为已读 (`PATCH /me/messages/{id}`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1035">_Mail.ReadWrite_: Mark a message read (`PATCH /me/messages/{id}`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1036">_Mail.Send_：发送邮件 (`POST /me/sendmail`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1036">_Mail.Send_: Send a message (`POST /me/sendmail`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1037">_MailboxSettings.ReadWrite_：更新用户的自动答复 (`PATCH /me/mailboxSettings`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1037">_MailboxSettings.ReadWrite_: Update the user's automatic reply (`PATCH /me/mailboxSettings`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1038">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1038">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1039">_Mail.Read_：从 bob@contoso.com 查找邮件 (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/messages?$filter=from/emailAddress/address eq 'bob@contoso.com'`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1039">_Mail.Read_: Find messages from bob@contoso.com (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/messages?$filter=from/emailAddress/address eq 'bob@contoso.com'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1040">_Mail.ReadWrite_：在名为“`Expense Reports`”的收件箱中新建文件夹 (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/mailfolders`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1040">_Mail.ReadWrite_: Create a new folder in the Inbox named `Expense Reports` (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/mailfolders`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1041">_Mail.Send_：发送邮件 (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/sendmail`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1041">_Mail.Send_: Send a message (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/sendmail`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1042">_MailboxSettings.Read_：获取用户邮箱的默认时区 (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/mailboxSettings/timeZone`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1042">_MailboxSettings.Read_: Get the default timezone for the user's mailbox (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/mailboxSettings/timeZone`)</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1043">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1043">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1065">注释</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1065">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1066">_Member.Read.Hidden_ 仅对工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1066">_Member.Read.Hidden_ is valid only on work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p155">可以隐藏某些 Office 365 组中的成员资格。这意味着只有该组的成员可以查看其成员。此功能可用于帮助遵守要求组织对外部用户（例如，表示某个班级内注册的学生的 Office 365 组）隐藏组成员身份的规定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p155">Membership in some Office 365 groups can be hidden. This means that only the members of the group can view its members. This feature can be used to help comply with regulations that require an organization to hide group membership from outsiders (for example, an Office 365 group that represents students enrolled in a class).</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1110">_Notes.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1110">_Notes.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_</span></span> |    <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1111">有限的笔记本访问权限（不推荐使用）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1111">Limited notebook access (deprecated)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1112">**不推荐使用**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1112">**Deprecated**</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p156">请勿使用。此权限不授予任何特权。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p156">Do not use. No privileges are granted by this permission.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1115">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1115">No</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1116">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1116">No</span></span>
