### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1130">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1130">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p157">_Notes.Read.All_ 和 _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ 仅适用于工作或学校帐户。所有其他权限对于 Microsoft 帐户和工作或学校帐户均有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p157">_Notes.Read.All_ and _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ are only valid for work or school accounts. All other permissions are valid for both Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1133">通过 _Notes.Create_ 权限，应用可以查看已登录用户的 OneNote 笔记本层次结构，并创建 OneNote 内容（笔记本、分区组、分区、页面等）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1133">With the _Notes.Create_ permission, an app can view the OneNote notebook hierarchy of the signed-in user and create OneNote content (notebooks, section groups, sections, pages, etc.).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1134">_Notes.ReadWrite_ 和 _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ 还允许应用修改针对已登录用户可以访问的 OneNote 内容的权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1134">_Notes.ReadWrite_ and _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ also allow the app to modify the permissions on the OneNote content that can be accessed by the signed-in user.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1135">对于工作或学校帐户，_Notes.Read.All_ 和 _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ 允许该应用访问已登录用户有权限在组织内访问的其他用户的 OneNote 内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1135">For work or school accounts, _Notes.Read.All_ and _Notes.ReadWrite.All_ allow the app to access other users' OneNote content that the signed-in user has permission to within the organization.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1136">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1136">Example usage</span></span>
#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1137">委托</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1137">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1138">_Notes.Create_：为登录用户新建笔记本 (`POST /me/onenote/notebooks`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1138">_Notes.Create_: Create a new notebooks for the signed-in user (`POST /me/onenote/notebooks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1139">_Notes.Read_：读取登录用户的笔记本 (`GET /me/onenote/notebooks`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1139">_Notes.Read_: Read the notebooks for the signed-in user (`GET /me/onenote/notebooks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1140">_Notes.Read.All_：获取登录用户有权在组织内访问的所有笔记本 (`GET /me/onenote/notebooks?includesharednotebooks=true`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1140">_Notes.Read.All_: Get all notebooks that the signed-in user has access to within the organization (`GET /me/onenote/notebooks?includesharednotebooks=true`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1141">_Notes.ReadWrite_：更新登录用户的页面 (`PATCH /me/onenote/pages/{id}/$value`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1141">_Notes.ReadWrite_: Update the page of the signed-in user (`PATCH /me/onenote/pages/{id}/$value`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1142">_Notes.ReadWrite.All_：在登录用户有权在组织内访问的其他用户笔记本中创建页面 (`POST /users/{id}/onenote/pages`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1142">_Notes.ReadWrite.All_: Create a page in another user's notebook that the signed-in user has access to within the organization (`POST /users/{id}/onenote/pages`).</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1143">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1143">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1144">_Notes.Read.All_：读取组中的所有用户笔记本 (`GET /groups/{id}/onenote/notebooks`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1144">_Notes.Read.All_: Read all users notebooks in a group (`GET /groups/{id}/onenote/notebooks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1145">_Notes.ReadWrite.All_：更新组织中任意用户的笔记本中的页面 (`PATCH /users/{id}/onenote/pages/{id}/$value`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1145">_Notes.ReadWrite.All_: Update the page in a notebook for any user in the organization (`PATCH /users/{id}/onenote/pages/{id}/$value`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1146">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1146">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1161">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1161">Example usage</span></span>
#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1162">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1162">Delegated</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1163">_Notifications.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_：发布以用户为中心的通知，然后可能会将该通知传递至用户运行在不同端点上的多个应用程序客户端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1163">_Notifications.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Publish a user-centric notification, which might then be delivered to the user’s multiple application clients running on different endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1164">(POST /me/notifications/)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1164">(POST /me/notifications/).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1181">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1181">Example usage</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1185">**注意**：创建[联机会议](/graph/api/application-post-onlinemeetings?view=graph-rest-beta)时，会代表在请求正文中指定的用户创建一个会议，但不会在该用户的日历上显示该会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1185">**Note**: Creating an [Online Meeting](/graph/api/application-post-onlinemeetings?view=graph-rest-beta) creates a meeting on behalf of a user specified in the request body, but does not show it on the user's Calendar.</span></span>

|:----------------|:------------------|:-------------|:-----------------------|:--------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1194">_email_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1194">_email_</span></span> |    <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1195">查看用户的电子邮件地址</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1195">View users' email address</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1196">允许应用读取用户的主电子邮件地址。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1196">Allows the app to read your users' primary email address.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1197">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1197">No</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1198">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1198">No</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1199">_offline_access_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1199">_offline_access_</span></span> |    <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1200">随时访问用户数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1200">Access user's data anytime</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1201">允许应用读取和更新用户数据，即使用户当前没有在使用此应用，也不例外。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1201">Allows the app to read and update user data, even when they are not currently using the app.</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1202">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1202">No</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1203">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1203">No</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1204">_openid_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1204">_openid_</span></span> |    <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1205">让用户登录</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1205">Sign users in</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1206">允许用户以其工作或学校帐户登录应用，并允许应用查看用户的基本个人资料信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1206">Allows users to sign in to the app with their work or school accounts and allows the app to see basic user profile information.</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1207">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1207">No</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1208">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1208">No</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1209">_个人资料_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1209">_profile_</span></span> |    <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1210">查看用户的基本个人资料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1210">View users' basic profile</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1211">允许应用查看用户的基本个人资料（名称、图片、用户名称）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1211">Allows the app to see your users' basic profile (name, picture, user name).</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1212">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1212">No</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1213">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1213">No</span></span> |

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1214">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1214">Application permissions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1215">无。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1215">None.</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1216">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1216">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p161">可以使用这些权限指定要在 Azure AD 授权和令牌请求中返回的项目。Azure AD v1.0 和 v2.0 终结点以不同的方式支持它们。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p161">You can use these permissions to specify artifacts that you want returned in Azure AD authorization and token requests. They are supported differently by the Azure AD v1.0 and v2.0 endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p162">使用 Azure AD (v1.0) 终结点时，仅使用 _openid_ 权限。在授权请求的 *scope* 参数中指定它，以在使用 OpenID Connect 协议让用户登录应用时返回 ID 令牌。有关详细信息，请参阅[使用 OpenID Connect 和 Azure Active Directory 来授权访问 Web 应用程序](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/develop/active-directory-protocols-openid-connect-code)。若要成功返回 ID 令牌，还必须确保在注册应用时已配置 _User.Read_ 权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p162">With the Azure AD (v1.0) endpoint, only the _openid_ permission is used. You specify it in the *scope* parameter in an authorization request to return an ID token when you use the OpenID Connect protocol to sign in a user to your app. For more information, see [Authorize access to web applications using OpenID Connect and Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/develop/active-directory-protocols-openid-connect-code). To successfully return an ID token, you must also make sure that the _User.Read_ permission is configured when you register your app.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p163">使用 Azure AD v2.0 终结点时，在 _scope_ 参数中指定 _offline\_access_ 权限，以在使用 OAuth 2.0 或 OpenID Connect 协议时显式请求获取刷新令牌。使用 OpenID Connect 时，指定 _openid_ 权限来请求获取 ID 令牌。还可指定 _email_ 权限和/或 _profile_ 权限，以在 ID 令牌中返回其他声明。使用 v2.0 终结点时，无需指定 _User.Read_ 来返回 ID 令牌。有关详细信息，请参阅 [OpenID Connect 作用域](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/develop/active-directory-v2-scopes#openid-connect-scopes)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p163">With the Azure AD v2.0 endpoint, you specify the _offline\_access_ permission in the _scope_ parameter to explicitly request a refresh token when using the OAuth 2.0 or OpenID Connect protocols. With OpenID Connect, you specify the _openid_ permission to request an ID token. You can also specify the _email_ permission, _profile_ permission, or both to return additional claims in the ID token. You do not need to specify _User.Read_ to return an ID token with the v2.0 endpoint. For more information, see [OpenID Connect scopes](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/develop/active-directory-v2-scopes#openid-connect-scopes).</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p164">**重要说明**：目前，Microsoft 身份验证库 (MSAL) 默认在授权和令牌请求中指定 _offline\_access_、_openid_、_profile_ 和 _email_。也就是说，在默认情况下，如果显式指定这些权限，Azure AD 可能会返回错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p164">**Important** The Microsoft Authentication Library (MSAL) currently specifies _offline\_access_, _openid_, _profile_, and _email_ by default in authorization and token requests. This means that, for the default case, if you specify these permissions explicitly, Azure AD may return an error.</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1298">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1298">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1299">_ProgramControl.Read.All_ 和 _ProgramControl.ReadWrite.All_ 仅对工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1299">_ProgramControl.Read.All_ and _ProgramControl.ReadWrite.All_ are valid only for work or school accounts.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1300">对于通过委派权限读取程序和程序控件的应用，登录的用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员、安全管理员、安全读取者或用户管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1300">For an app with delegated permissions to read programs and program controls, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator, Security Administrator, Security Reader or User Administrator.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1301">对于通过委派权限写入程序和程序控件的应用，登录的用户必须是以下管理员角色之一的成员：全局管理员、安全管理员、安全读取者或用户管理员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1301">For an app with delegated permissions to write programs and program controls, the signed-in user must be a member of one of the following administrator roles: Global Administrator or User Administrator.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1302">若要详细了解管理员角色，请参阅[在 Azure Active Directory 中分配管理员角色](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1302">For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1328">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1328">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1329">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1329">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1330">_Reports.Read.All_：读取电子邮件应用程序在 7 天内的使用情况详情报告 (`GET /reports/EmailAppUsage(view='Detail',period='D7')/content`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1330">_Reports.Read.All_: Read usage detail report of email apps with period of 7 days (`GET /reports/EmailAppUsage(view='Detail',period='D7')/content`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1331">_Reports.Read.All_：读取电子邮件在日期“2017-01-01”的的活动详情报告 (`GET /reports/EmailActivity(view='Detail',data='2017-01-01')/content`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1331">_Reports.Read.All_: Read activity detail report of email with date of '2017-01-01' (`GET /reports/EmailActivity(view='Detail',data='2017-01-01')/content`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1332">_Reports.Read.All_：读取 Office 365 激活详情报告 (`GET /reports/Office365Activations(view='Detail')/content`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1332">_Reports.Read.All_: Read Office 365 activations detail report (`GET /reports/Office365Activations(view='Detail')/content`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1333">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1333">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1396">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1396">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-and-application"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1397">委派和应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1397">Delegated and Application</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1398">_SecurityEvents.Read.All_：从对租户可用的所有许可安全提供程序中读取所有安全警报的列表 (`GET /beta/security/alerts`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1398">_SecurityEvents.Read.All_: Read the list of all security alerts from all licensed security providers available to your tenant (`GET /beta/security/alerts`)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1399">_SecurityEvents.ReadWrite.All_：更新或读取对租户可用的所有许可安全提供程序中的安全警报 (`PATCH /beta/security/alerts/{id}`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1399">_SecurityEvents.ReadWrite.All_: Update or read security alerts from all licensed security providers available to your tenant  (`PATCH /beta/security/alerts/{id}`)</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1450">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1450">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1451">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1451">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1452">_Sites.Read.All_：读取 SharePoint 根网站上的列表 (`GET /v1.0/sites/root/lists`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1452">_Sites.Read.All_: Read the lists on the SharePoint root site (`GET /v1.0/sites/root/lists`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1453">_Sites.ReadWrite.All_：在 SharePoint 列表中新建列表项 (`POST /v1.0/sites/root/lists/123/items`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1453">_Sites.ReadWrite.All_: Create new list items in a SharePoint list (`POST /v1.0/sites/root/lists/123/items`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1454">_Sites.Manage.All_：将新列表添加到 SharePoint 网站 (`POST /v1.0/sites/root/lists`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1454">_Sites.Manage.All_: Add a new list to a SharePoint site (`POST /v1.0/sites/root/lists`)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1455">_Sites.FullControl.All_：对 SharePoint 网站和列表的完全访问权限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1455">_Sites.FullControl.All_: Complete access to SharePoint sites and lists.</span></span>

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1483">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1483">Application permissions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1484">无。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1484">None.</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1485">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1485">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p174">_任务_权限用于控制对 Outlook 任务的访问权限。Microsoft Planner 任务的访问权限由[_组_权限](#group-permissions)控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p174">_Tasks_ permissions are used to control access for Outlook tasks. Access for Microsoft Planner tasks is controlled by [_Group_ permissions](#group-permissions).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p175">目前仅工作或学校帐户支持_共享_权限。即使具有_共享_权限，如果未授予拥有共享内容的用户在文件夹内修改内容访问用户权限，读取和写入仍会失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p175">_Shared_ permissions are currently only supported for work or school accounts. Even with _Shared_ permissions, reads and writes may fail if the user who owns the shared content has not granted the accessing user permissions to modify content within the folder.</span></span>

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1490">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1490">Example usage</span></span>
#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1491">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1491">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1492">_Tasks.Read_：获取用户邮箱中的所有任务 (`GET /me/outlook/tasks`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1492">_Tasks.Read_: Get all tasks in a user's mailbox (`GET /me/outlook/tasks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1493">_Tasks.Read.Shared_：在文件夹中访问组织中其他用户与你共享的任务 (`Get /users{id|userPrincipalName}/outlook/taskfolders/{id}/tasks`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1493">_Tasks.Read.Shared_: Access tasks in a folder shared to you by another user in your organization (`Get /users{id|userPrincipalName}/outlook/taskfolders/{id}/tasks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1494">_Tasks.ReadWrite_：将事件添加到用户的默认任务文件夹 (`POST /me/outlook/tasks`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1494">_Tasks.ReadWrite_: Add an event to the user's default task folder (`POST /me/outlook/tasks`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1495">_Tasks.Read_：获取用户邮箱中的所有未完成任务 (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks?$filter=status ne 'completed'`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1495">_Tasks.Read_: Get all uncompleted tasks in a user's mailbox (`GET /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks?$filter=status ne 'completed'`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1496">_Tasks.ReadWrite_：更新用户邮箱中的任务 (`PATCH /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks/id`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1496">_Tasks.ReadWrite_: Update a task in a user's mailbox (`PATCH /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks/id`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1497">_Tasks.ReadWrite.Shared_：代表其他用户完成任务 (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks/id/complete`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1497">_Tasks.ReadWrite.Shared_: Complete a task on behalf of another user (`POST /users/{id | userPrincipalName}/outlook/tasks/id/complete`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1498">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1498">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1500">委派权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1500">Delegated permissions</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1526">注解</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1526">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1527">上述所有权限仅对工作或学校帐户有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1527">All the permissions above are valid only for work or school accounts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1528">若要使应用能够阅读或编写委派权限的所有协议或协议接受情况，登录用户必须分配有全局管理员、条件访问管理员或安全管理员角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1528">For an app to read or write all agreements or agreement acceptances with delegated permissions, the signed-in user must be assigned the Global Administrator, Conditional Access Administrator or Security Administrator role.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1529">若要详细了解管理员角色，请参阅[在 Azure Active Directory 中分配管理员角色](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1529">For more information about administrator roles, see [Assigning administrator roles in Azure Active Directory](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/active-directory/active-directory-assign-admin-roles).</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1534">_Agreement.ReadWrite.All_：阅读和编写所有使用条款协议 (`POST /beta/agreements`)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1534">_Agreement.ReadWrite.All_: Read and write all terms of use agreements (`POST /beta/agreements`)</span></span>

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1609">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1609">Application permissions</span></span>

|   <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1610">权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1610">Permission</span></span>    |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1611">显示字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1611">Display String</span></span>   |  <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1612">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1612">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1613">需经过管理员同意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1613">Admin Consent Required</span></span> |
|:----------------|:------------------|:-------------|:-----------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1614">_User.Read.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1614">_User.Read.All_</span></span> |    <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1615">读取所有用户的完整个人资料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1615">Read all users' full profiles</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1616">允许应用在没有登录用户的情况下读取组织中其他用户的整套个人资料属性、组成员身份、下属和经理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1616">Allows the app to read the full set of profile properties, group membership, reports and managers of other users in your organization, without a signed-in user.</span></span>| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1617">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1617">Yes</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1618">_User.ReadWrite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1618">_User.ReadWrite.All_</span></span> |   <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1619">读取和写入所有用户的完整个人资料</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1619">Read and write all users' full profiles</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p181">允许应用在没有登录用户的情况下读取和写入组织中其他用户的整套个人资料属性、组成员身份、下属和经理。还允许应用创建和删除非管理用户。不允许重置用户密码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p181">Allows the app to read and write the full set of profile properties, group membership, reports and managers of other users in your organization, without a signed-in user.  Also allows the app to create and delete non-administrative users. Does not allow reset of user passwords.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1623">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1623">Yes</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1624">_User.Invite.All_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1624">_User.Invite.All_</span></span>  |     <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1625">将来宾用户邀请到组织</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1625">Invite guest users to the organization</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1626">允许应用无需具有已登录用户即可将来宾用户邀请到你的组织。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1626">Allows the app to invite guest users to your organization, without a signed-in user.</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1627">可访问</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1627">Yes</span></span> |

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1632">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1632">Remarks</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p182">通过 _User.Read_ 权限，应用还可以通过 [organization](/graph/api/resources/organization?view=graph-rest-1.0) 资源读取工作或学校帐户的已登录用户的基本公司信息。以下属性可用：ID、displayName 和 verifiedDomains。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p182">With the _User.Read_ permission, an app can also read the basic company information of the signed-in user for a work or school account through the [organization](/graph/api/resources/organization?view=graph-rest-1.0) resource. The following properties are available: id, displayName, and verifiedDomains.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p183">对于工作或学校帐户，完整个人资料包括 [User](/graph/api/resources/user?view=graph-rest-1.0) 资源的所有声明属性。在读取时，默认情况下仅返回有限数量的属性。若要读取不在默认设置中的属性，请使用 `$select`。默认属性包括：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p183">For work or school accounts, the full profile includes all of the declared properties of the [User](/graph/api/resources/user?view=graph-rest-1.0) resource. On reads, only a limited number of properties are returned by default. To read properties that are not in the default set, use `$select`. The default properties are:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1639">displayName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1639">displayName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1640">givenName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1640">givenName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1641">jobTitle</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1641">jobTitle</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1642">mail</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1642">mail</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1643">mobilePhone</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1643">mobilePhone</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1644">officeLocation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1644">officeLocation</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1645">preferredLanguage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1645">preferredLanguage</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1646">surname</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1646">surname</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1647">userPrincipalName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1647">userPrincipalName</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1648">_User.ReadWrite_ 和 _User.Readwrite.All_ 委派权限允许应用更新工作或学校帐户的以下配置文件属性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1648">_User.ReadWrite_ and _User.Readwrite.All_ delegated permissions allow the app to update the following profile properties for work or school accounts:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1649">aboutMe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1649">aboutMe</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1650">birthday</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1650">birthday</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1651">hireDate</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1651">hireDate</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1652">interests</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1652">interests</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1653">mobilePhone</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1653">mobilePhone</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1654">mySite</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1654">mySite</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1655">pastProjects</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1655">pastProjects</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1656">photo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1656">photo</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1657">preferredName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1657">preferredName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1658">responsibilities</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1658">responsibilities</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1659">schools</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1659">schools</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1660">skills</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1660">skills</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1661">通过 _User.ReadWrite.All_ 应用程序权限，应用可更新工作或学校帐户的所有声明属性，但密码除外。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1661">With the _User.ReadWrite.All_ application permission, the app can update all of the declared properties of work or school accounts except for password.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1662">要读取或写入工作或学校帐户的直接下属 (`directReports`) 或经理 (`manager`)，应用必须具有 _User.Read.All_（只读）或 _User.ReadWrite.All_。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1662">To read or write direct reports (`directReports`) or the manager (`manager`) of a work or school account, the app must have either _User.Read.All_ (read only) or _User.ReadWrite.All_.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p184">_User.ReadBasic.All_ 权限限制应用访问称为基本个人资料的有限属性集。这是因为完整的个人资料可能包含敏感的目录信息。基本个人资料仅包括以下属性：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p184">The _User.ReadBasic.All_ permission constrains app access to a limited set of properties known as the basic profile. This is because the full profile might contain sensitive directory information. The basic profile includes only the following properties:</span></span> 

- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1666">displayName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1666">displayName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1667">givenName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1667">givenName</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1668">mail</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1668">mail</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1669">photo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1669">photo</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1670">surname</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1670">surname</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1671">userPrincipalName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1671">userPrincipalName</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p185">若要读取用户的组成员资格 (`memberOf`)，则应用必须具有 [_Group.Read.All_](#group-permissions) 或 [_Group.ReadWrite.All_](#group-permissions)。但是，如果用户还具有 [directoryRole](/graph/api/resources/directoryrole?view=graph-rest-1.0) 或 [administrativeUnit](/graph/api/resources/administrativeunit?view=graph-rest-beta) 中的成员资格，则应用还将需要有效权限来读取这些资源，否则 Microsoft Graph 将返回错误。这意味着应用还需要[目录权限](#directory-permissions)，而对于委派权限来说，已登录的用户还需要组织内的足够特权来访问目录角色和管理单元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p185">To read the group memberships of a user (`memberOf`), the app must have either [_Group.Read.All_](#group-permissions) or [_Group.ReadWrite.All_](#group-permissions). However, if the user also has membership in a [directoryRole](/graph/api/resources/directoryrole?view=graph-rest-1.0) or an [administrativeUnit](/graph/api/resources/administrativeunit?view=graph-rest-beta), the app will need effective permissions to read those resources too, or Microsoft Graph will return an error. This means the app will also need [Directory permissions](#directory-permissions), and, for delegated permissions, the signed-in user will also need sufficient privileges in the organization to access directory roles and administrative units.</span></span> 

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1675">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1675">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1676">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1676">Delegated</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1677">_User.Read_：读取登录用户的完整配置文件 (`GET /me`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1677">_User.Read_: Read the full profile for the signed-in user (`GET /me`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1678">_User.ReadWrite_：更新登录用户的照片 (`PUT /me/photo/$value`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1678">_User.ReadWrite_: Update the photo of the signed-in user (`PUT /me/photo/$value`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1679">_User.ReadBasic.All_：查找名称以“David”开头的所有用户 (`GET /users?$filter=startswith(displayName,'David')`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1679">_User.ReadBasic.All_: Find all users whose name starts with "David" (`GET /users?$filter=startswith(displayName,'David')`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1680">_User.Read.All_：读取用户的经理 (`GET /user/{id | userPrincipalName}/manager`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1680">_User.Read.All_: Read a user's manager (`GET /user/{id | userPrincipalName}/manager`).</span></span>


#### <a name="application"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1681">应用程序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1681">Application</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1682">_User.Read.All_：通过 delta 查询读取所有用户和关系 (`GET /beta/users/delta?$select=displayName,givenName,surname`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1682">_User.Read.All_: Read all users and relationships through delta query (`GET /beta/users/delta?$select=displayName,givenName,surname`).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1683">_User.ReadWrite.All_：更新组织中任意用户的照片 (`PUT /user/{id | userPrincipalName}/photo/$value`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1683">_User.ReadWrite.All_: Update the photo for any user in the organization (`PUT /user/{id | userPrincipalName}/photo/$value`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1684">有关涉及多个权限的更复杂的情况，请参阅[权限方案](#permission-scenarios)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1684">For more complex scenarios involving multiple permissions, see [Permission scenarios](#permission-scenarios).</span></span>

## <a name="user-activity-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1685">用户活动权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1685">User Activity permissions</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1692">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1692">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1693">将应用活动读取和写入到用户的活动源</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1693">Read and write app activity to users' activity feed</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1694">允许应用读取和报告登录用户在应用中的活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1694">Allows the app to read and report the signed-in user's activity in the app.</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1695">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1695">No</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1696">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1696">Yes</span></span> |

#### <a name="application-permissions"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1697">应用程序权限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1697">Application permissions</span></span>

### <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1699">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1699">Remarks</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1700">*UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp* 对 Microsoft 帐户和工作或学校帐户均有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1700">*UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp* is valid for both Microsoft accounts and work or school accounts.</span></span> 
 
<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1701">与此权限相关联的 *CreatedByApp* 约束指示服务将基于调用应用的标识（MSA 应用 ID 或针对跨平台应用程序标识配置的一组应用 ID）对结果应用隐式筛选。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1701">The *CreatedByApp* constraint associated with this permission indicates the service will apply implicit filtering to results based on the identity of the calling app, either the MSA app id or a set of app ids configured for a cross-platform application identity.</span></span> 

### <a name="example-usage"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1702">用法示例</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1702">Example usage</span></span>

#### <a name="delegated"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1703">委派</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1703">Delegated</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1704">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_：基于最后一天发布的相关联的历史记录项来获取最近特定用户活动的列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1704">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Get a list of recent unique user activities based on associated history items published in the last day.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1705">(GET /me/activities/recent)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1705">(GET /me/activities/recent).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1706">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_：发布或更新可能由应用程序用户恢复的用户活动。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1706">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Publish or update a user activity which may be resumed by the user of the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1707">(PUT /me/activities/%2Farticle%3F12345)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1707">(PUT /me/activities/%2Farticle%3F12345).</span></span>
*   <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1708">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_：发布或更新指定用户活动的历史记录项，以表示用户参与的时间段。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1708">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Publish or update a history item for a specified user activity in order to represent the period of user engagement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1709">(PUT /me/activities/{id}/historyItems/{id})。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1709">(PUT /me/activities/{id}/historyItems/{id}).</span></span>
*   <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1710">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_：根据用户发起的请求删除用户活动或删除无效数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1710">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Delete a user activity in response to user initiated request or to remove invalid data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1711">(DELETE /me/activities/{id})。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1711">(DELETE /me/activities/{id}).</span></span>
*   <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1712">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_：根据用户发起的请求删除历史记录项或删除无效数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1712">_UserActivity.ReadWrite.CreatedByApp_: Delete a history item in response to user initiated request or to remove invalid data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1713">(DELETE /me/activities/{id}/historyItems/{id})。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1713">(DELETE /me/activities/{id}/historyItems/{id}).</span></span>

## <a name="permission-scenarios"></a><span data-ttu-id="eeadf-1714">权限方案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-1714">Permission scenarios</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="eeadf-p191">本节介绍一些面向组织中 [user](/graph/api/resources/user?view=graph-rest-1.0) 和 [group](/graph/api/resources/group?view=graph-rest-1.0) 资源的常见方案。这些表显示了应用执行方案要求的特定操作所需的权限。请注意，在某些情况下，应用执行特定操作的能力取决于权限是应用程序权限还是委派权限。如果是委派权限，应用的有效权限还将取决于组织内已登录用户的特权。有关详细信息，请参阅[委派权限、应用程序权限和有效权限](./auth/auth-concepts#microsoft-graph-permissions)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="eeadf-p191">This section shows some common scenarios that target [user](/graph/api/resources/user?view=graph-rest-1.0) and [group](/graph/api/resources/group?view=graph-rest-1.0) resources in an organization. The tables show the permissions that an app needs to be able to perform specific operations required by the scenario. Note that in some cases the ability of the app to perform specific operations will depend on whether a permission is an application or delegated permission. In the case of delegated permissions, the app's effective permissions will also depend on the privileges of the signed-in user within the organization. For more information, see  [Delegated permissions, Application permissions, and effective permissions](./auth/auth-concepts#microsoft-graph-permissions).</span></span>
